\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_CliDbGetAlwaysUseImsApn()}{Mtc\_CliDbGetAlwaysUseImsApn()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Cli\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Cli\+Db\+Get\+Always\+Use\+Ims\+Apn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Get the use ims apn mode when available. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em -\/1} & Indications the device shall never use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS. \\
\hline
{\em 0} & Indications The device shall use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS when the device\textquotesingle{}s internet access is using cellular coverage. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & Indications the device shall always use the I\+MS A\+PN for R\+CS whenever it is in cellular coverage, even if non-\/cellular access is available.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

Get rcs disable state. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 1,the} & client is rcs enable. \\
\hline
{\em 0,the} & client is temporarily disabled. \\
\hline
{\em -\/1,the} & client is permanently disabled. \\
\hline
{\em -\/2,the} & client is permanently disabled, but user triggered events result in an attempt to re-\/enable the client. \\
\hline
{\em -\/3,the} & client is placed in dormant state.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_CliDbSetApplyChange()}{Mtc\_CliDbSetApplyChange()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static int com.\+juphoon.\+cmcc.\+app.\+lemon.\+Mtc\+Cli\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Cli\+Db\+Set\+Apply\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{boolean}]{b\+Apply }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Set data change apply flag realtime. If data change apply flag is true, below db set functions(ex \mbox{\hyperlink{classcom_1_1juphoon_1_1cmcc_1_1app_1_1lemon_1_1_mtc_cli_db_adab39f721ce71460f813c993efbf6044}{Mtc\+Cli\+Db.\+Mtc\+\_\+\+Cli\+Db\+Set\+User\+Name}}) will apply change immediately. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em Mtc\+Common\+Constants\+::\+Z\+OK} & Set data change apply flag successfully. \\
\hline
